data_integration.py
```python
'''  
Handles data integration from MachForms to Google Sheets.  
'''  
import gspread  
from google.oauth2.service_account import Credentials  
import requests  
class DataIntegration:  
    def __init__(self):  
        self.credentials = Credentials.from_service_account_file('path/to/credentials.json')  
        self.gc = gspread.authorize(self.credentials)  
        self.sheet_name = "MasterRecord"  # Replace with your Google Sheets name  
        self.machform_urls = [  
            "https://machform1.com/api/view",  
            "https://machform2.com/api/view",  
            "https://machform3.com/api/view"  
        ]  
        self.api_keys = [  
            "machform_api_key_1",  
            "machform_api_key_2",  
            "machform_api_key_3"  
        ]  
    def fetch_data(self):  
        '''  
        Fetches data from MachForms using their API.  
        '''  
        all_data = []  
        for url, api_key in zip(self.machform_urls, self.api_keys):  
            headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"}  
            response = requests.get(url, headers=headers)  
            if response.status_code == 200:  
                all_data.extend(response.json())  
            else:  
                print(f"Failed to fetch data from {url}. Status code: {response.status_code}")  
        return all_data  
    def update_google_sheets(self, data):  
        '''  
        Updates Google Sheets with fetched data.  
        '''  
        try:  
            sheet = self.gc.open(self.sheet_name).sheet1  
            # Clear existing data  
            sheet.clear()  
            # Assuming data is a list of dictionaries  
            headers = list(data[0].keys())  
            sheet.append_row(headers)  
            for record in data:  
                sheet.append_row(list(record.values()))  
            print("Google Sheets updated successfully.")  
        except Exception as e:  
            print(f"Error updating Google Sheets: {e}")  
```

academic_pathway_generator.py
```python
'''
Generates personalized academic pathways using OpenAI API.
'''
import openai
class AcademicPathwayGenerator:
    def __init__(self, api_key):
        '''
        Initializes the AcademicPathwayGenerator with the OpenAI API key.
        '''
        openai.api_key = api_key
    def generate_pathway(self, student_data):
        '''
        Generates an academic pathway for a student using the OpenAI API.
        Parameters:
        student_data (dict): A dictionary containing student information.
        Returns:
        dict: A dictionary containing the generated academic pathway.
        '''
        prompt = self.create_prompt(student_data)
        response = openai.Completion.create(
            engine="text-davinci-003",
            prompt=prompt,
            max_tokens=150
        )
        pathway = response.choices[0].text.strip()
        return {"student_id": student_data["student_id"], "pathway": pathway}
    def create_prompt(self, student_data):
        '''
        Creates a prompt for the OpenAI API based on student data.
        Parameters:
        student_data (dict): A dictionary containing student information.
        Returns:
        str: A prompt string for the OpenAI API.
        '''
        prompt = (
            f"Generate a personalized academic pathway for a student with the following details:\n"
            f"Name: {student_data['name']}\n"
            f"Interests: {student_data['interests']}\n"
            f"Previous Academic Performance: {student_data['performance']}\n"
            f"Goals: {student_data['goals']}\n"
            f"Provide a detailed academic plan."
        )
        return prompt
```

document_handler.py
```python
'''
Manages Google Docs template filling and PDF export.
'''
from pydrive.auth import GoogleAuth
from pydrive.drive import GoogleDrive
from googleapiclient.discovery import build
from googleapiclient.http import MediaFileUpload
import os
class DocumentHandler:
    def __init__(self):
        '''
        Initializes the DocumentHandler with Google Drive authentication.
        '''
        self.gauth = GoogleAuth()
        self.gauth.LocalWebserverAuth()
        self.drive = GoogleDrive(self.gauth)
        self.docs_service = build('docs', 'v1', credentials=self.gauth.credentials)
        self.drive_service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=self.gauth.credentials)
    def fill_template(self, pathway_data, template_id):
        '''
        Fills a Google Docs template with pathway data.
        Parameters:
        pathway_data (dict): A dictionary containing pathway information.
        template_id (str): The ID of the Google Docs template.
        Returns:
        str: The ID of the filled document.
        '''
        # Create a copy of the template
        copy_title = f"{pathway_data['student_id']}_Academic_Pathway"
        copy_metadata = {'name': copy_title}
        copied_file = self.drive_service.files().copy(fileId=template_id, body=copy_metadata).execute()
        doc_id = copied_file['id']
        # Fill the template with pathway data
        requests = [
            {'replaceAllText': {
                'containsText': {'text': '{{student_name}}', 'matchCase': True},
                'replaceText': pathway_data['name']
            }},
            {'replaceAllText': {
                'containsText': {'text': '{{academic_pathway}}', 'matchCase': True},
                'replaceText': pathway_data['pathway']
            }}
        ]
        self.docs_service.documents().batchUpdate(documentId=doc_id, body={'requests': requests}).execute()
        return doc_id
    def export_to_pdf(self, doc_id, output_path):
        '''
        Exports a Google Docs document to PDF.
        Parameters:
        doc_id (str): The ID of the Google Docs document.
        output_path (str): The file path to save the PDF.
        '''
        request = self.drive_service.files().export_media(fileId=doc_id, mimeType='application/pdf')
        with open(output_path, 'wb') as pdf_file:
            pdf_file.write(request.execute())
        print(f"Document exported to PDF at {output_path}.")
```

email_sender.py
```python
'''
Sends emails to students with the generated PDF.
'''
import smtplib
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart
from email.mime.text import MIMEText
from email.mime.application import MIMEApplication
import os
class EmailSender:
    def __init__(self, smtp_server, smtp_port, username, password):
        '''
        Initializes the EmailSender with SMTP server details and login credentials.
        '''
        self.smtp_server = smtp_server
        self.smtp_port = smtp_port
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
    def send_email(self, recipient_email, pdf_path):
        '''
        Sends an email with the attached PDF to the specified recipient.
        Parameters:
        recipient_email (str): The email address of the recipient.
        pdf_path (str): The file path to the PDF to be attached.
        '''
        try:
            # Create a multipart message
            msg = MIMEMultipart()
            msg['From'] = self.username
            msg['To'] = recipient_email
            msg['Subject'] = "Your Personalized Academic Pathway"
            # Add body to email
            body = "Please find attached your personalized academic pathway."
            msg.attach(MIMEText(body, 'plain'))
            # Open the PDF file in binary mode
            with open(pdf_path, "rb") as attachment:
                # Add file as application/octet-stream
                part = MIMEApplication(attachment.read(), _subtype="pdf")
                part.add_header('Content-Disposition', 'attachment', filename=os.path.basename(pdf_path))
                msg.attach(part)
            # Connect to the server and send the email
            with smtplib.SMTP(self.smtp_server, self.smtp_port) as server:
                server.starttls()  # Secure the connection
                server.login(self.username, self.password)
                server.send_message(msg)
            print(f"Email sent successfully to {recipient_email}.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to send email to {recipient_email}. Error: {e}")
```

salesforce_handler.py
```python
'''
Stores student records in Salesforce.
'''
from simple_salesforce import Salesforce
class SalesforceHandler:
    def __init__(self, username, password, security_token):
        '''
        Initializes the SalesforceHandler with Salesforce credentials.
        '''
        self.sf = Salesforce(username=username, password=password, security_token=security_token)
    def store_record(self, student_data):
        '''
        Stores student records in Salesforce.
        Parameters:
        student_data (dict): A dictionary containing student information.
        Returns:
        dict: A dictionary containing the result of the Salesforce operation.
        '''
        try:
            # Assuming there is a custom object in Salesforce named 'Student__c'
            student_record = {
                'Name': student_data['name'],
                'Email__c': student_data['email'],
                'Interests__c': student_data['interests'],
                'Performance__c': student_data['performance'],
                'Goals__c': student_data['goals'],
                'Pathway__c': student_data['pathway']
            }
            result = self.sf.Student__c.create(student_record)
            print("Student record stored successfully in Salesforce.")
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error storing student record in Salesforce: {e}")
            return None
```

admin_interface.py
```python
'''
Provides a tracking interface for admins.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk
class AdminInterface:
    def __init__(self):
        self.tree = None
    def display_dashboard(self, root):
        '''
        Displays the admin dashboard with tracking interface.
        Parameters:
        root (tk.Tk): The root Tkinter window.
        '''
        frame = ttk.Frame(root)
        frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
        # Create a Treeview widget for displaying student records
        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(frame, columns=("Student ID", "Name", "Email", "Pathway"), show="headings")
        self.tree.heading("Student ID", text="Student ID")
        self.tree.heading("Name", text="Name")
        self.tree.heading("Email", text="Email")
        self.tree.heading("Pathway", text="Pathway")
        self.tree.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
        # Add a scrollbar
        scrollbar = ttk.Scrollbar(frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.tree.yview)
        self.tree.configure(yscroll=scrollbar.set)
        scrollbar.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
        # Load initial data into the Treeview
        self.load_data()
    def load_data(self):
        '''
        Loads student data into the Treeview widget.
        '''
        # Example data, replace with actual data fetching logic
        student_data = [
            {"student_id": "001", "name": "Alice", "email": "alice@example.com", "pathway": "Engineering"},
            {"student_id": "002", "name": "Bob", "email": "bob@example.com", "pathway": "Arts"},
            {"student_id": "003", "name": "Charlie", "email": "charlie@example.com", "pathway": "Science"}
        ]
        for student in student_data:
            self.tree.insert("", "end", values=(student["student_id"], student["name"], student["email"], student["pathway"]))
    def update_data(self, new_data):
        '''
        Updates the Treeview with new student data.
        Parameters:
        new_data (list): A list of dictionaries containing student information.
        '''
        # Clear existing data
        for item in self.tree.get_children():
            self.tree.delete(item)
        # Insert new data
        for student in new_data:
            self.tree.insert("", "end", values=(student["student_id"], student["name"], student["email"], student["pathway"]))
```

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

## 📖 Documentation

Please see [here](https://python.langchain.com) for full documentation on:

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

- How-To examples (demos, integrations, helper functions)

- Reference (full API docs)

- Resources (high-level explanation of core concepts)

# Student Evaluation Automation Software

This software automates the evaluation process for incoming students by integrating data from MachForms into Google Sheets, generating personalized academic pathways using the OpenAI API, filling a branded Google Docs template, exporting the result as a PDF, emailing it to the student, storing it in Salesforce, and providing a tracking interface for admins.

## Main Functions

1. **Data Integration**: Fetches student data from MachForms and updates it into a Google Sheets master record.
2. **Academic Pathway Generation**: Uses the OpenAI API to generate personalized academic pathways based on student data.
3. **Document Handling**: Fills a Google Docs template with the generated pathway and exports it as a PDF.
4. **Email Sending**: Sends the generated PDF to students via email.
5. **Salesforce Storage**: Stores student records in Salesforce for future reference.
6. **Admin Interface**: Provides a dashboard for admins to track and manage student records.

## Installation

### Environment Setup

1. **Python Installation**: Ensure Python 3.x is installed on your system. You can download it from [python.org](https://www.python.org/downloads/).

2. **Virtual Environment**: It is recommended to use a virtual environment to manage dependencies. You can create one using:
   ```bash
   python -m venv venv
   source venv/bin/activate  # On Windows use `venv\Scripts\activate`
   ```

3. **Install Dependencies**: Install the required Python packages using pip:
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

   The `requirements.txt` file should include:
   ```plaintext
   gspread
   google-auth
   openai
   pydrive
   google-api-python-client
   simple-salesforce
   requests
   ```

### API Keys and Credentials

- **Google API Credentials**: Obtain a `credentials.json` file from the Google Cloud Console for accessing Google Sheets and Google Docs.
- **OpenAI API Key**: Sign up at [OpenAI](https://openai.com/) and obtain an API key.
- **Salesforce Credentials**: Ensure you have a Salesforce account with API access and obtain the necessary credentials (username, password, security token).

## Usage

1. **Configure API Keys and Credentials**: Update the `main.py` file with your API keys and credentials:
   - Replace `your_openai_api_key_here` with your OpenAI API key.
   - Update email and Salesforce credentials in the respective sections.

2. **Run the Application**: Execute the main application file to start the program:
   ```bash
   python main.py
